< Review>
I love going to H&M lots of deals on clothing for adults and kids. I haven't entered this Palmdale location before but decided to stop by for some clothes seeing that they had great prices on clothing. The reason I give this store a 3 is because the employees need to be a bit more welcoming and smile more. Out of all the employees working there was about 2 that were cheery and happy. The rest were very serious and didn't seem approachable. They looked at us like if we were going to take something from the store but wouldn't approach us to see  if we needed help. But other then that store is well kept and aisles are easy to walk around.< /Review>

02/03/2021 - From arrival to departure - a first time experience with Dr Rad and her staff. I was experiencing sudden constant double vision for 9 days -  on 02/02 my neuro opthalmogist said to get out of glasses with monovision and get regular glasses where both eyes look far or near at the same time. I needed new glasses ASAP. Dr Rad's office has a lab on premise.  I was told when I made appointment that I would possibly be able to get my glasses within 2-3 hours on same day. On 02/03 I arrived 15 minutes earlier as advised to complete paperwork. I was seen on time. My visit with Dr Rad was exceptional. She precribed prism lenses and if my vision shifted I could return in 30 days and she would replace lenses at no charge. I am scheduled for an MRI and Dr Rad said if my vision needed additional adfjustment within 60 days due to medical findings she would be flexible with extending the 30 day policy. My appointment was at noon, I left at about 1pm and was sent a text at 236pm that my glasses were ready. Needless to say, the new glasses prescribed by Dr Rad worked  immediately - my double vision was gone.

With no reservations, I highly recommend Dr Rad. I have multiple eye issues and have seen several eye doctors over a span of 60+ years, her precision to prescribe the prism lenses and explain "double vision' was calming and gave me peace of mind.< /Text>

<Text>I just stood in line waiting for parts and overheard Angel J telling a customer he can't use synthetic oil and go back to conventional oil.  This misinformation is severely flawed taken as an absolute.  It is perfectly safe to switch between synthetic and conventional oils provided your engine seals and gaskets are healthy.  Synthetic oil provides better protection but has more aggressive detergents that clean your engine better BUT potentially expose gasket and seal failure.  Bottom line, any leaks are ultimately caused by old/faulty seals and gaskets.  As long as your engine is't leaking any oil, use what oil you please and/or fits your budget.  Simply make sure it's the proper viscosity for your engine.</Text><Pictures>None<//Pictures>< Date>
